–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä –æ—Ç gpt –Ω–∞ fsm
class Character {
  constructor() {
    this.position = { x: 10, y: 0 }; // –°–ø–∞–≤–Ω –Ω–∞ 10 –∫–ª–µ—Ç–æ–∫ —Å–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∞
    this.facing = "left"; // –†–∞–∑–≤–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –ª–∏—Ü–æ–º –∫ —Å—Ç—É–¥–∏–∏
    this.sitting = false;
  }

  execute(command) {
    switch (command) {
      case "walkToChair":
        this.moveToChair();
        break;

      case "teleport":
        this.position = { x: "behindCurtain", y: "studio" };
        this.execute("walkToChair");
        break;

      case "sitDown":
        this.playAnimation("sit_1", () => this.execute("sitting"));
        break;

      case "sitting":
        this.loopAnimation("sit_2", () => !this.sitting, "standUp");
        break;

      case "standUp":
        this.playAnimation("stand_up", () => this.execute("walkOut"));
        break;

      case "walkOut":
        this.moveToExit();
        break;

      case "despawn":
        console.log("Character removed");
        break;
    }
  }

  moveToChair() {
    if (this.position.x === "offscreen") {
      this.execute("teleport");
    } else if (this.position.x === "chair") {
      this.execute("sitDown");
    } else {
      this.position.x -= 1; // –î–≤–∏–≥–∞–µ–º—Å—è –∫ —Å—Ç—É–ª—É
      setTimeout(() => this.execute("walkToChair"), 100);
    }
  }

  moveToExit() {
    if (this.position.x === 10) {
      this.execute("despawn");
    } else {
      this.position.x += 1; // –î–≤–∏–≥–∞–µ–º—Å—è –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ
      setTimeout(() => this.execute("walkOut"), 100);
    }
  }

  playAnimation(name, onComplete) {
    console.log(`Playing ${name}`);
    setTimeout(onComplete, 1000);
  }

  loopAnimation(name, condition, nextCommand) {
    console.log(`Looping ${name}`);
    if (condition()) {
      this.execute(nextCommand);
    } else {
      setTimeout(() => this.loopAnimation(name, condition, nextCommand), 1000);
    }
  }
}

class MyError extends AggregateError {
  constructor(
      message,
      cause,
      ... errors
  ) {
      
      super( errors, message, { cause } )
      this.errors = errors
      const desc = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor( this, 'stack' )
      const stack_get = desc?.get ?? ( ()=> super.stack ?? desc?.value )

      Object.defineProperty( this, 'stack', {
    get: ()=> ( stack_get.call( this ) ?? super.stack ?? this.message ) + '\n' + [ JSON.stringify( this.cause, null, '  ' ) ?? 'no cause', ... this.errors.map( e => e.stack ) ].map(
        e => e.trim()
      .replace( /at /gm, '   at ' )
      .replace( /^(?!    +at )(.*)/gm, '    at | $1 (#)' )
    ).join('\n')
      } )
  }
}
